Happy T.G.I.F,

As it stands, we have a total number of 50 delegates that have fully paid for our L.E.A.D.S‚Äô21 Youth Conference. The retreat centre is on our necks to confirm the total number of delegates attending the conference so they can make accommodation arrangements, we are delaying this confirmation till Sunday for persons who have promised to pay on or before Sunday the 9th of May, 2021.

I am sending this message out just incase there are persons who are planning to pay after Sunday. Please note that we are not the only youth body using the retreat centre during that period and once we confirm the total number of delegates to the Administrator of the centre, we will not be able to add any more delegates. Please and please, if anyone pays after this Sunday, your money would be duly refunded to you as no arrangement for accommodation would be made for you and you will not be able to go with us to the conference. 

I am sending this lengthy message out on time to avoid stories that touch. This is beyond the committee. Everyone should take note and inform their friends and colleagues. 

Thanks and God bless.

Linda Obi
